</span><span class="token php language-php"></span><span class="token php language-php" style="color: rgb(64, 120, 242);">session_destroy</span><span class="token php language-php" style="color: rgb(56, 58, 66);">(</span><span class="token php language-php" style="color: rgb(56, 58, 66);">)</span><span class="token php language-php" style="color: rgb(56, 58, 66);">;</span><span class="token php language-php">
</span><span class="token php language-php"></span><span class="token php language-php" style="color: rgb(64, 120, 242);">header</span><span class="token php language-php" style="color: rgb(56, 58, 66);">(</span><span class="token php language-php double-quoted-string" style="color: rgb(80, 161, 79);">"Location: index.php"</span><span class="token php language-php" style="color: rgb(56, 58, 66);">)</span><span class="token php language-php" style="color: rgb(56, 58, 66);">;</span><span class="token php language-php">
</span><span class="token php language-php"></span><span class="token php language-php" style="color: rgb(166, 38, 164);">exit</span><span class="token php language-php" style="color: rgb(56, 58, 66);">;</span><span class="token php language-php">
</span><span class="token php language-php"></span><span class="token php language-php delimiter" style="color: rgb(228, 86, 73);">?&gt;</span></code></pre></div></div></li></ol><hr style="margin-top: 3em; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Secure Passwords</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Always hash passwords using </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-1my065n r-z2wwpe r-114j4xv r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">password_hash()</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Input Validation</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Sanitize and validate all user inputs to prevent SQL injection and XSS attacks.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System;
